wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for buried prefixed tags
buried:wikidata and buried:wikipedia tags link to a different objects, because buried:wikipedia tag points to a redirect that should be followed
Q61260 vs (missing) article redirects from de:Gustav Gründgens to de:Gustaf Gründgens
Gründgens Gustav - an affected OSM element that may be improved

overpass query usable in JOSM that will load all objects where this specific error is present:
[out:xml][timeout:3600]; ( node(2098725035)['buried:wikidata'='Q61260']['buried:wikipedia'='de:Gustav Gründgens']; ); (._;>;); out meta qt;//['wikipedia wikidata mismatch - follow wikipedia redirect - for buried prefixed tags']
